grass in fedora-32

This page displays detail informations of the grass package. You might want go back to the main page of grass.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-03-03 Sandro Mani - 7.8.2-3 - Rebuild (gdal)
2020-01-29 Fedora Release Engineering - 7.8.2-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2019-12-12 Markus Neteler - 7.8.2 - new upstream version GRASS GIS 7.8.2
2019-10-24 Markus Neteler - 7.8.1 - new upstream version GRASS GIS 7.8.1 - it supports GDAL 3 and PROJ 6
2019-10-24 Markus Neteler - 7.8.0-5 - fix EPEL7 support
2019-09-23 Markus Metz - 7.8.0-4 - enable bzip2 compression
2019-09-20 Markus Neteler - 7.8.0-3 - added missing proj-datumgrid and proj-datumgrid-world for >= F30 - fix create symlink to unversioned name
2019-09-14 Elliot C. Lee - 7.8.0-2 - patch for upstream package and SPEC file
2019-09-13 Markus Neteler - 7.8.0-1 - new upstream version of GRASS GIS 7.8.0 - dropped outdated liblas dependency
2019-08-14 Markus Neteler - 7.8.0-RC1 - test version of GRASS GIS 7.8.0RC1 with Python 3 support - removal of no longer required Python 2/3 shebang update
